diff --git a/harper-core/src/linting/flaunt_flout.rs b/harper-core/src/linting/flaunt_flout.rs
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..94c6e95
--- /dev/null
+++ b/harper-core/src/linting/flaunt_flout.rs
@@ -0,0 +1,170 @@
+use crate::{
+    Lint, Token,
+    expr::{Expr, SequenceExpr},
+    linting::{ExprLinter, LintKind, Suggestion, expr_linter::Chunk},
+};
+
+pub struct FlauntFlout {
+    expr: SequenceExpr,
+}
+
+impl Default for FlauntFlout {
+    fn default() -> Self {
+        // Match "flaunt" (and inflected forms) followed by words related to rules/laws,
+        // with optional intervening non-rule/law words.
+        let rule_words = &[
+            "law", "laws", "rule", "rules", "regulation", "regulations",
+            "convention", "conventions", "standard", "standards",
+            "protocol", "protocols", "code", "codes",
+            "norm", "norms", "guideline", "guidelines",
+        ];
+
+        Self {
+            expr: SequenceExpr::word_set(&["flaunt", "flaunted", "flaunting", "flaunts"])
+                .t_ws()
+                .then_zero_or_more(|tok: &Token, src: &[char]| {
+                    if tok.kind.is_word() {
+                        let word = tok.span.get_content_string(src).to_lowercase();
+                        !rule_words.contains(&word.as_str())
+                    } else {
+                        !tok.kind.is_word()
+                    }
+                })
+                .then_word_set(rule_words),
+        }
+    }
+}
+
+impl ExprLinter for FlauntFlout {
+    type Unit = Chunk;
+
+    fn expr(&self) -> &dyn Expr {
+        &self.expr
+    }
+
+    fn match_to_lint(&self, toks: &[Token], src: &[char]) -> Option<Lint> {
+        let verb_span = toks.first()?.span;
+        let verb_chars = verb_span.get_content(src);
+
+        enum Form {
+            Base,
+            Past,
+            Ing,
+            ThirdPerson,
+        }
+
+        let infl = match verb_chars.last().map(|c| c.to_ascii_lowercase()) {
+            Some('t') => Form::Base,
+            Some('d') => Form::Past,
+            Some('g') => Form::Ing,
+            Some('s') => Form::ThirdPerson,
+            _ => return None,
+        };
+
+        Some(Lint {
+            span: verb_span,
+            lint_kind: LintKind::WordChoice,
+            suggestions: vec![Suggestion::replace_with_match_case_str(
+                match infl {
+                    Form::Base => "flout",
+                    Form::Past => "flouted",
+                    Form::Ing => "flouting",
+                    Form::ThirdPerson => "flouts",
+                },
+                verb_chars,
+            )],
+            message: "`Flaunt` means to show off. Did you mean `flout` (to openly disregard)?".to_string(),
+            ..Default::default()
+        })
+    }
+
+    fn description(&self) -> &str {
+        "Looks for `flaunt` wrongly used when `flout` (to openly disregard rules) is intended."
+    }
+}
+
+#[cfg(test)]
+mod tests {
+    use crate::linting::{flaunt_flout::FlauntFlout, tests::{assert_lint_count, assert_suggestion_result}};
+
+    #[test]
+    fn correct_flaunted_laws() {
+        assert_suggestion_result(
+            "He flaunted US bankruptcy laws for personal gain.",
+            FlauntFlout::default(),
+            "He flouted US bankruptcy laws for personal gain.",
+        );
+    }
+
+    #[test]
+    fn correct_flaunts_rules() {
+        assert_suggestion_result(
+            "It's got a Kirk-esque captain who flaunts the rules in favour of 'getting her done'.",
+            FlauntFlout::default(),
+            "It's got a Kirk-esque captain who flouts the rules in favour of 'getting her done'.",
+        );
+    }
+
+    #[test]
+    fn correct_flaunting_laws() {
+        assert_suggestion_result(
+            "That's what deranged scientists flaunting the laws of God and Man are for.",
+            FlauntFlout::default(),
+            "That's what deranged scientists flouting the laws of God and Man are for.",
+        );
+    }
+
+    #[test]
+    fn correct_flaunt_rules() {
+        assert_suggestion_result(
+            "some seem to flaunt the basic rules of punctuation and grammar.",
+            FlauntFlout::default(),
+            "some seem to flout the basic rules of punctuation and grammar.",
+        );
+    }
+
+    #[test]
+    fn correct_flaunt_the_law() {
+        assert_suggestion_result(
+            "He decided to flaunt the law.",
+            FlauntFlout::default(),
+            "He decided to flout the law.",
+        );
+    }
+
+    #[test]
+    fn correct_flaunting_regulations() {
+        assert_suggestion_result(
+            "Companies were flaunting safety regulations.",
+            FlauntFlout::default(),
+            "Companies were flouting safety regulations.",
+        );
+    }
+
+    #[test]
+    fn dont_flag_correct_flaunt() {
+        assert_lint_count(
+            "She loves to flaunt her wealth at parties.",
+            FlauntFlout::default(),
+            0,
+        );
+    }
+
+    #[test]
+    fn dont_flag_correct_flaunting() {
+        assert_lint_count(
+            "He was flaunting his new car in front of everyone.",
+            FlauntFlout::default(),
+            0,
+        );
+    }
+
+    #[test]
+    fn dont_flag_flaunt_style() {
+        assert_lint_count(
+            "She flaunted her unique style at the gala.",
+            FlauntFlout::default(),
+            0,
+        );
+    }
+}

+use crate::{
+    Lint, Token,
+    expr::{Expr, SequenceExpr},
+    linting::{ExprLinter, LintKind, Suggestion, expr_linter::Chunk},
+};
+
+pub struct FlauntFlout {
+    expr: SequenceExpr,
+}
+
+impl Default for FlauntFlout {
+    fn default() -> Self {
+        // Match "flaunt" (and inflected forms) followed by words related to rules/laws,
+        // with optional intervening non-rule/law words.
+        let rule_words = &[
+            "law", "laws", "rule", "rules", "regulation", "regulations",
+            "convention", "conventions", "standard", "standards",
+            "protocol", "protocols", "code", "codes",
+            "norm", "norms", "guideline", "guidelines",
+        ];
+
+        Self {
+            expr: SequenceExpr::word_set(&["flaunt", "flaunted", "flaunting", "flaunts"])
+                .t_ws()
+                .then_zero_or_more(|tok: &Token, src: &[char]| {
+                    if tok.kind.is_word() {
+                        let word = tok.span.get_content_string(src).to_lowercase();
+                        !rule_words.contains(&word.as_str())
+                    } else {
+                        !tok.kind.is_word()
+                    }
+                })
+                .then_word_set(rule_words),
+        }
+    }
+}
+
+impl ExprLinter for FlauntFlout {
+    type Unit = Chunk;
+
+    fn expr(&self) -> &dyn Expr {
+        &self.expr
+    }
+
+    fn match_to_lint(&self, toks: &[Token], src: &[char]) -> Option<Lint> {
+        let verb_span = toks.first()?.span;
+        let verb_chars = verb_span.get_content(src);
+
+        enum Form {
+            Base,
+            Past,
+            Ing,
+            ThirdPerson,
+        }
+
+        let infl = match verb_chars.last().map(|c| c.to_ascii_lowercase()) {
+            Some('t') => Form::Base,
+            Some('d') => Form::Past,
+            Some('g') => Form::Ing,
+            Some('s') => Form::ThirdPerson,
+            _ => return None,
+        };
+
+        Some(Lint {
+            span: verb_span,
+            lint_kind: LintKind::WordChoice,
+            suggestions: vec![Suggestion::replace_with_match_case_str(
+                match infl {
+                    Form::Base => "flout",
+                    Form::Past => "flouted",
+                    Form::Ing => "flouting",
+                    Form::ThirdPerson => "flouts",
+                },
+                verb_chars,
+            )],
+            message: "`Flaunt` means to show off. Did you mean `flout` (to openly disregard)?".to_string(),
+            ..Default::default()
+        })
+    }
+
+    fn description(&self) -> &str {
+        "Looks for `flaunt` wrongly used when `flout` (to openly disregard rules) is intended."
+    }
+}
+
+#[cfg(test)]
+mod tests {
+    use crate::linting::{flaunt_flout::FlauntFlout, tests::{assert_lint_count, assert_suggestion_result}};
+
+    #[test]
+    fn correct_flaunted_laws() {
+        assert_suggestion_result(
+            "He flaunted US bankruptcy laws for personal gain.",
+            FlauntFlout::default(),
+            "He flouted US bankruptcy laws for personal gain.",
+        );
+    }
+
+    #[test]
+    fn correct_flaunts_rules() {
+        assert_suggestion_result(
+            "It's got a Kirk-esque captain who flaunts the rules in favour of 'getting her done'.",
+            FlauntFlout::default(),
+            "It's got a Kirk-esque captain who flouts the rules in favour of 'getting her done'.",
+        );
+    }
+
+    #[test]
+    fn correct_flaunting_laws() {
+        assert_suggestion_result(
+            "That's what deranged scientists flaunting the laws of God and Man are for.",
+            FlauntFlout::default(),
+            "That's what deranged scientists flouting the laws of God and Man are for.",
+        );
+    }
+
+    #[test]
+    fn correct_flaunt_rules() {
+        assert_suggestion_result(
+            "some seem to flaunt the basic rules of punctuation and grammar.",
+            FlauntFlout::default(),
+            "some seem to flout the basic rules of punctuation and grammar.",
+        );
+    }
+
+    #[test]
+    fn correct_flaunt_the_law() {
+        assert_suggestion_result(
+            "He decided to flaunt the law.",
+            FlauntFlout::default(),
+            "He decided to flout the law.",
+        );
+    }
+
+    #[test]
+    fn correct_flaunting_regulations() {
+        assert_suggestion_result(
+            "Companies were flaunting safety regulations.",
+            FlauntFlout::default(),
+            "Companies were flouting safety regulations.",
+        );
+    }
+
+    #[test]
+    fn dont_flag_correct_flaunt() {
+        assert_lint_count(
+            "She loves to flaunt her wealth at parties.",
+            FlauntFlout::default(),
+            0,
+        );
+    }
+
+    #[test]
+    fn dont_flag_correct_flaunting() {
+        assert_lint_count(
+            "He was flaunting his new car in front of everyone.",
+            FlauntFlout::default(),
+            0,
+        );
+    }
+
+    #[test]
+    fn dont_flag_flaunt_style() {
+        assert_lint_count(
+            "She flaunted her unique style at the gala.",
+            FlauntFlout::default(),
+            0,
+        );
+    }
+}
